size="3">Smith &amp; Wesson &nbsp; &nbsp;Made in the USA</font></h2> <p>M&amp;P15 Sport II</p> <p>America's most popular sporting rifle is now back and better than ever! The new M&amp;P15 Sport II retains all of the features that made the original M&amp;P15 Sport great, now with the addition of a dust cover, forward assist and <span>Armornite® Finish.&nbsp;</span></p> <p><span>The M&amp;P15 Sport II also features a detachable 30 round magazine, adjustable A2 post front sight with adjustable dual aperture rear sight, 16" 4140 steel 1:9 twist barrel, single stage trigger, forged internal trigger guard, hard coat black anodized receiver finish, chromed firing pin, high-temp polymer handguard, six-position telescoping stock, and an A2 birdcage style flash suppressor.&nbsp;</span></p> <p>With the stock collapsed, the gun has an overall length of 32" (35" with the stock extended).</p> <p>The new M&amp;P15 Sport II rifle joins Smith &amp; Wesson's popular line of M&amp;P15 semi-automatic tactical rifles. With it's ready-to-go design, the M&amp;P15 Sport II benefits from accurate rifling, adjustable sights and a single stage trigger.&nbsp;</p> <p>Versatile, modular and an exceptional value, the M&amp;P15 Sport II rifle is a perfect choice for everyone from brand new shooters, to the tactical rifle enthusiast!&nbsp;</p> <p> <object width="520" height="380"
